There are several kinds of bread and fried noodles, and a chef cooks wontons. This is why everyone would rather queue up to eat in the main restaurant. I have been to many parent-child hotels, including Disneyland and other parent-child hotels in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. As for breakfast, it was very crowded and was arranged in the executive floor hall of Huibao. The food was almost exactly the same as in the main restaurant, with both Chinese and Western dishes made fresh. The Ultraman experience is particularly poor, except for children who like it. Everyone understands it. The price is not proportional to the facilities and services. The hygiene is not very good. The white cup on the tea table has orange and orange fruit bits stained in it. The black cup is all gray. The key is the Ultraman themed family hotel. There is no Ultraman in the TV series and animations, but the Disney hotels are all Disney animations. The decor and furniture smell particularly bad. Don't waste your money, everyone.
